Preparations for Establishing a Great Hebei Library in Northern Henan

Central Committee Member Zhang Ji Helps Collect Books (Xinxiang Correspondence) People in Henan Province, in order to promote social education and save cultural decline, planned to establish a large-scale Hebei Library in the autumn of last year, located in Xinxiang, the center of northern Henan, which has received sympathy and assistance from all sectors of society. The library's preparation situation is described below.

Famous People Initiate The initiators of the library number more than 150. In addition to people from Henan Province and those related to Henan Province who are happy to participate, many people from all sides who sympathize with the library's proposition have also joined one after another, striving to support it. Zhang Ji, Shang Zhen, Zhang Fang, Liu Zhenhua, Qi Zhenru, Li Wenhao, Li Da, Xu Xinwu, Zhang Guangyu, Zhang Tianfang, Guo Zhonghuai, Tian Xiaoxiang, and Yang Yifeng are all central figures in actively supporting it.

A Glimpse of the Organization The library's preparatory committee is the highest organ of the library, officially established on February 15th of this year. The chairman is Mr. Hu Yu, the special commissioner of the Fourth District. Under the preparatory committee, there are also fundraising, book collection, and construction committees, responsible for fundraising, book collection, and construction respectively.

Preparation Plan The outline of the library's preparation plan has been approved by the general assembly. It has very detailed designs for popularizing education and improving culture. The library's colleagues deeply feel that the drawbacks of today's school system are hindering the progress of ordinary people and obliterating the individuality of students. They plan to adopt the advantages of the old academy system and reorganize it to adapt to modern trends. However, due to financial constraints, they will temporarily use the library as a base point, and take restoring the spirit of the old academy system as their goal, proceeding in stages, hoping to complete the entire project within seven years.

Raising Huge Sums of Money After the fundraising began, Mr. Liu Jingfu, the chairman of the province, immediately donated a large sum to show his leadership. Subsequently, with the enthusiastic donations from all sectors of society and entrepreneurs from various places, more than 20,000 yuan has been raised, with the business community providing the strongest support. For example, the staff of Tongheyu and other firms automatically donated more than 1,000 yuan in just a few days, which can be described as enthusiastic about education. According to the library staff, the most diligent fundraisers this time are Zhang Fang, Li Wenhao, Li Da, Hu Yuwei, Wang Yanqing, Guo Zhonghuai, and Yang Yifeng. The remaining fundraising committee members are still actively soliciting donations, and it is heard that a large number of donations will still be received soon. As soon as the experts have drawn the design drawings, construction will begin on the new library base on West Street in Xinxiang City.

Zhang Ji Collects Books The chairman of the library's book collection committee is Central Committee Member Zhang Ji. Mr. Zhang is the earliest initiator of the library and is most concerned about the preparation matters. Currently, the book collection work has been actively started. In addition to the initiators Tian Xiaoxiang, Guo Zhonghuai, Yang Yifeng, and others generously donating all of their family's book collections accumulated over generations, the Xinxiang Education Bureau has also transferred more than 5,000 volumes of Ming Dynasty Buddhist scriptures to the library for safekeeping. The total number of volumes has exceeded 20,000. A few days ago, Chairman Zhang Ji returned to Xinxiang from Beijing, and during his spare time, he sent letters to domestic cultural organizations, central ministries and departments, and publishing circles, asking them to donate as much as possible. It is heard that many places are donating all of their valuable publications. Therefore, the registration and thank-you work of the library's collection group is extremely busy. In the future, when the new library is completed, Henan's cultural organizations will have another new force.

Li Ximou, Commissioner for Educational Inspection in Europe, Reports on Vocational Education in Various Countries

Vocational Education Takes Elementary Education as Its Foundation, Elementary Schools Must Have Wood and Metal Workshops. Our Country Should Establish Vocational Education with Several Years of Skill Training in the Later Stages of Elementary School. On April 24, at the Ministry of Education's Commemorative Week, Li Ximou, who returned from inspecting Europe, reported on the issue of vocational education. The scope of vocational education, its breadth, has no fixed definition. In its broad sense, all school courses that emphasize vocational training can be called vocational education, such as the training of lawyers in university law departments, the training of engineers in engineering departments, and the training of teachers in normal schools, all can be called vocational education. In its narrow sense, it can be limited to the education and training of manufacturing and daily necessities artisans, such as carpenters, shoemakers, tailors, etc. Modern vocational education in Europe, although it does not include university specialty training and normal school education, commercial schools and agricultural schools are indeed recognized as a type of vocational education. Therefore, the so-called vocational education actually includes commercial, agricultural, and miscellaneous occupational education and training. In the past, professions in our country were also divided into categories, forming a separate line or industry. Within a line or industry, there were also business methods and craft skills, but their organization and habits were mostly based on apprenticeship, without school education and training in the theory of various industries. Therefore, there were professions, but no so-called vocational education. Vocational skills were only passed down between masters and apprentices. Before the 19th century, the situation in Europe was similar to that in our country, with apprenticeship and no so-called vocational education. However, since the industrial revolution in the 19th century, family handicrafts have gradually been eliminated, and the use of machines has expanded day by day. Ordinary workers, without considerable training, cannot cope with the complexity of machine construction and the skillful use of machines. As various manufacturing industries have developed day by day, they all want to sell their products in the world market. Therefore, in order to seek progress in skills and reduce costs, for these reasons, the rise of vocational teaching in Europe was a natural result. The underdevelopment of vocational education in our country to this day is also due to these reasons. The manufacturing industry is not developed, or the products are not sought to be sold in the world market, there is no competition in skills, so there is no need for vocational education. At a minimum, domestic manufacturers have not yet seen this. The facilities for vocational education in various European countries are quite uneven, because each country has different social conditions, habits, and educational systems. In terms of nature, there are vocational continuation schools and vocational specialty schools. Vocational continuation schools are specially established for young employees in factories, firms, etc. Most European countries have laws stipulating that all young men and women under the age of 18 who are employed must attend continuation schools. These courses are either taught at night, three times a week, totaling about eight to ten hours, or taught during the day. All clear-headed factory owners and shopkeepers know that increasing the knowledge of their employees can directly increase their efficiency in service, so they are happy to let their employees study in vocational continuation schools, and some even allow them to take continuation classes during working hours without deducting their salaries. Vocational specialty schools are schools where students are completely taught in schools, and advanced vocational schools. All young men and women must attend vocational continuation schools after completing compulsory education and taking up employment, or seek further education and enter secondary schools, or take up vocational training and enter junior vocational schools. Those who enter advanced vocational schools must have studied in secondary schools to the sixth grade, and sometimes must have practical experience. Among the countries visited by this educational inspection group, Germany and France can represent the facilities for vocational education in continental Europe. The British vocational education system is similar to that of continental countries. The Soviet Union focuses on agricultural and industrial training, so its system is also more special. The division of subjects in various types of schools depends on their level and nature. For example, in vocational continuation schools, all entrants are already employed, so the subjects taught mainly focus on supplementing the students' theoretical knowledge of their professions. Junior vocational schools are for the training of craftsmen in various manufacturing industries, so the classification is very detailed, such as shop assistants, typists, bookkeepers, carpenters, masons, shoemakers, tailors, blacksmiths, jewelers, cabinetmakers, engravers, printers, bookbinders, photographers, designers, weavers, knitters, embroiderers, and housework, even barbers and waiters. In the city of Hamburg, Germany, there are a total of 70 lines, and in Vienna, Austria, there are 90 lines. Advanced vocational schools are all for the training of engineering and advanced manufacturing personnel, such as civil engineering, architectural engineering, electrical engineering, chemical engineering, manufacturing engineering, as well as senior commercial and agricultural personnel. The British vocational continuation education has junior vocational education classes, taught either in the evening or during the day. Junior vocational schools include junior industrial, junior commercial, junior agricultural, and junior art schools. In terms of advanced vocational schools, there are specialized higher vocational schools. However, British vocational schools generally emphasize the theory of vocational training, while practical training in the profession is still undertaken by factories or shops. This is one of the most significant differences from continental European countries.

In continental Europe, the so-called vocational schools must emphasize both theory and workshop work, and sometimes even emphasize workshop work. When students are practicing in the workshop, the time spent on their work, the quantity of raw materials, and the value of the finished products must be recorded and examined, so as to resemble the workshop system. It seems that when students leave school and enter factories for employment, there will be no separation and unfamiliarity. Russian vocational education focuses on the training of the agricultural and industrial classes, so its facilities are not like those of England, nor are they like the continental European system. Within factories, there are often joint schools, mostly with night classes. There are preliminary industrial knowledge classes, divided into twenty lessons, specially designed for workers without engineering knowledge. There are special youth classes, specially designed for the children of workers who have graduated from elementary schools. The teaching time is from April to half a year. There are youth industrial classes, designed for middle school graduates. There are worker classes, designed to train workers who already have skills. The teaching time is from two to two and a half years. There are worker colleges, specially designed to prepare workers for university, with a teaching time of four years. The situation in Russia, where workers lack school education, is quite similar to that in our country, so its facilities for vocational continuing education and training seem to offer many points of reference. There are not many vocational schools in Denmark, but the Arts and Crafts College in Copenhagen has an electrical engineering department that can be graduated in ten days, a steamship and fishing boat driving and repair department that can be graduated in two weeks, an automotive engineering department that can be graduated in ten weeks, and an internal combustion engine department, including automobiles, airplanes, and machines, that can be graduated in ten weeks. There are also blacksmithing, metalworking, iron bed, woodworking, and cabinetmaking departments, with graduation periods ranging from two weeks to ten weeks. The internal facilities are extremely complete, and students can obtain sufficient practical experience. It is also a special school for vocational training. Here, one point that must be supplemented is that in various types of vocational schools in European countries, in addition to vocational subjects, common sense, such as civic education, the national language, and physical education training, are all compulsory subjects. From this regulation, it can be seen that European countries attach great importance to national education. However, vocational education is still based on elementary education, so the success or failure of vocational education is greatly related to elementary education. In European countries, elementary schools must have wood and metal workshops. Students in the fifth, sixth, and seventh grades of elementary school practice woodworking, metalworking, and the use of machines in stages. Therefore, all elementary school graduates already have considerable craft knowledge and skills. If our country wants to establish vocational education, especially in industrial vocational education, the

starting point may still be the skill training of students in the later years of elementary school.

Recent Work of the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education

(Nanchang Correspondence) The Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education has implemented many reorganizations and plans for the province's education cause in the past two months. The news obtained is compiled as follows:

Registration of Education Bureau Director Candidates According to the recently revised Education Bureau Organization Regulations, new methods have been established. All personnel who have the qualifications stipulated in the regulations will be reviewed and registered by the department at any time, and interviews will be conducted. Those deemed qualified will be announced and ordered to county governments to be appointed as needed.

Organizing a Correspondence Research Institute for Elementary School Teachers Gathering teachers from across the province to participate in research, divided into two types: reading books and correspondence discussions. The books to be read are designated by the institute, and discussion questions are raised by the participants at any time. The research program is divided into three terms, each school term being one term. A correspondence examination method is also used. Those who pass the examination may be exempted from part or all of the teacher certification examination in the future.

Reorganizing Local Education Establishing Important Considerations for Reorganizing Local Education in Various Counties, with 34 articles in total. 14 items on education administration, 15 items on elementary school education, and 5 items on social education. These were printed into a booklet and distributed to various counties for compliance. Another 10 Important Considerations for County Magistrates in Managing Local Education were specially designed to urge county magistrates to pay special attention to education.

Preparing Summer Schools and Educational Achievement Exhibition Divided into four groups: academic education, local education administration, elementary education, and music and physical education. Educational experts from inside and outside the province are invited to serve as lecturers. The summer school will be opened this summer vacation, and all preparations are underway. At the same time, an educational achievement exhibition will be held, collecting educational administration achievements from various places for observation, and inviting lecturers to criticize and guide.

Actively Preparing for Holding Graduation Examinations for Middle and Primary Schools Middle school examinations will be held by district, divided into six districts: Nanchang, Shangrao, Linchuan, Yichun, and Jiujiang. The provincial capital's elementary school examinations are hosted by the Department of Education. This year is the second time. All elementary schools in other counties have been ordered to comply, and the examinations are hosted by the county education bureaus. Detailed examination methods and scoring methods have also been established.

Promoting Music Education A special committee has been organized, and music expert Cheng Maojun has been appointed as the chairman to plan everything. Currently, they are engaged in the investigation and improvement of old and new dramas and songs, and plan to create folk wedding and funeral music scores. In schools, lyrics for "Revival," "Saving the Country," and "Movement" have been produced and distributed to schools for practice and singing.

Editing the Education Guidance Series The department's Education Design Committee is responsible for editing and translating the guidance series. The completed volumes include: Outline of Vocational Guidance, Testing Theory and Practice, and Must-Knows for Managing Local Education.

Intensifying Military Training in Senior High Schools Another Military Education Committee has been organized in Nanjing. Committee members have personally inspected the implementation of military education in all schools above senior high school, assessed the results, reported them in detail to the Department of Education, and the department has strictly ordered the schools to improve separately based on the inspection opinions.

Chu Hui Seng Discusses the Difficulty of Independent Education Funding

Russian Boxer Indemnity Funds Encounter Problems, Peking University's Finances Affected and Difficult to Maintain. Boxer Indemnity Funds Have Been Diverted Elsewhere, Cultural Undertakings Can Only Use Interest. The Joint Association of University Faculty and Staff, in order to safeguard the independent education funding movement, specially appointed Cai Yuanpei, Chu Minyi, Zhang Xiangyong, Zheng Hongnian, and Zhu Hui Seng, etc., to liaise with the government and relevant parties, to ensure the independence of education funding at all times and in all matters. A reporter from the "Shen Shi" newspaper specially visited Mr. Chu at his residence, and was granted an interview. The reporter first inquired about the progress plan of the case. Mr. Chu replied that although the association had elected colleagues to plan the event, it had not yet received a formal notification, and even after the notification arrives, the association has not yet decided whether to accept it, given the complexity of the case. When asked about the current financial situation of the various schools, Mr. Chu replied that Peking University was originally maintained by the Russian Boxer Indemnity, but now that the funds have encountered problems, there is a great concern that it cannot be maintained. As for the British Boxer Indemnity, according to the agreement, it should also be used for cultural undertakings, but most of it has now been transferred and diverted by the Ministry of Railways, and the rest has been borrowed by the Huai River Guidance Association. In terms of culture, only the interest can be used in the future, and it is still doubtful whether the interest can be received monthly. When asked about the representatives who have been recommended, even if they have not yet accepted the recommendation of the association, what is your individual opinion on this matter, Mr. Chu replied that it is difficult to decide on this matter before discussion. However, the only way out is still to find a way within the return of the Boxer Indemnity from various countries, otherwise, even if we liaise with the government and relevant parties, it will be difficult to achieve the goal in fact.

Amateur Group A Pistol Shooting

Sino-Portuguese Master Finals First Day Li Gongying Plays

The Opponent is Medina

5:30 PM and 9:15 PM

First Match 1000 Points, 500 Points Each Before and After

The two leading figures in the Shanghai amateur pistol shooting world are the Chinese "Pistol King" Li Gongying and the Portuguese Medina. The two have met in the Shanghai amateur Group A pistol shooting finals four times. In 1930, the first time they met, Li defeated the Portuguese to win the championship. In 1931 and 1932, the Portuguese won twice and won the championship. This time will be their fourth encounter. These two Sino-Portuguese masters have their own merits. Judging from the usual situation, Li can certainly gain the upper hand, but in formal competitions, unexpected facts often occur due to psychological changes, so it should be treated differently from usual. Regardless of who wins or loses this time, in terms of skill alone, the two have reached the pinnacle, which is indeed the most interesting and exciting scene in the whole game. The final consists of a total of 2,000 points, divided into three days. The first to reach the full score wins. Today is the first day with two matches, each with 500 points, at 5:30 PM and 9:15 PM at the Amateur Pistol Shooting Association inside the Lianhua General Association at No. 3 Beijing Road. The admission ticket for each match is one yuan.

Essays

National Flower

— Chi Fo

How beautiful the flowers are; using flowers to represent a country is called a (national flower), which is especially beautiful and lovely. Because the magnificent land is as beautiful and lovely as a flower, people cannot but love this (national flower) that represents the country. In the past, the Chinese people's love for flowers differed; Tao Yuanming loved chrysanthemums, saying they were flowers of recluses; Zhou Shulin loved lotus flowers, saying they were flowers of gentlemen; Lin Hejing loved plum blossoms, even treating them as his wife; Pi Rixiu loved peach blossoms, also calling them beauties. Nowadays, people are different, blinded by fame and fortune, who doesn't desire wealth? It's not just friends who say (dying under a peony flower is worth it, even as a ghost), but advocate that this flower of wealth! The peony! Should be the national flower, opposing plum and chrysanthemum as the national flower. The world is so turbulent, and most people's minds are like this, which shows our (national character).

England uses the rose as its national flower, and France uses the lily as its national flower, both bearing the colors of commemoration or representation of national character. Only Japan actually uses the cherry blossom as its national flower. In the early summer of the island nation, cherry blossoms are gorgeous. They call it the (Cherry Blossom Festival), which is very lively. In fact, cherry blossoms are even more frivolous than peach blossoms. They cannot withstand wind and rain, nor can they endure cold. The period of showing off is very short. Is this the shadow of the violent sun? Moreover, their cherry blossoms have flowers but no fruit; they have appearance but cannot be eaten. Isn't this a sign of hatred for goods? As early summer approaches, wheat shows its green ears, and cherry blossoms adorn the red trees. It is their season of pride. Unfortunately, once the plum rain season arrives and lotus flowers emerge from the water, of course a burst of red will pass away, and the flowers will fall and people will die. Who will bury the flowers?

I heard that the Japanese regard sorghum as the national flower of the puppet state, which is really wishful thinking. Sorghum flowers, what beauty do they have that can be a national flower? But sorghum can be squeezed to make wine. Aren't the Japanese treating the three northeastern provinces as sorghum, squeezing their people's fat and oil? It's a pity that a bunch of puppet state monarchs, ministers, generals, and soldiers are dreaming their golden dream every day and refuse to wake up. Using sorghum as the national flower is not as good as simply using (golden dream) as the national flower!

Hometown

— Hua Ling

Recently, in various literary publications, apart from (peeling cocoons) patriotic remarks and disguised (sister, I love you), the most fashionable are (returning home ○○) and (hometown ○○) articles. That's right, this kid also has a hometown. This kid's hometown also occupies a considerable position on this earth. This kid's hometown, although not Suzhou or Hangzhou, which are famous all over the world, nor the Eight Character Bridge or Xiao Chang Temple, which were made famous by the Imperial Army, but it has the same people, dogs, crows, bedbugs, local tyrants and evil gentry, local ruffians, free-loving girls, and farmers who go bankrupt in good years.

Although this kid hasn't returned to his hometown for three years, the green mountains that woodcutters cut down every day and the green water that citizens drink and wash their chamber pots with haven't tasted the flavor of the enemy's iron hooves. I think they haven't changed color. The five-foot wide (main street) where (a sedan chair passes by in the street, and three-foot infants also stand guard) I think still maintains its antique charm, (China's inherent culture).

The large and small earthen mounds that the declining poets admired, as mentioned by the new scholars, I think have made a lot of progress in quantity in the past few years. Poets and writers, after seeing the endless (tomb landscape), may have (A Night Visit to the Tomb) and other (immortal works) included in (Eating, Sleeping, Playing with Women's Leftovers). If the modern futurist painters see the scene of (widows sweeping graves), they may produce a (cone and curve) to be displayed at the French (Spring Salon), which will definitely leave a good impression on Westerners of the Chinese people.

The wheelbarrow may still have the supreme authority to instill culture, no, there are also sailboats, which can be said to be evenly divided. Quinine to fight malaria and smallpox medicine to extinguish tiger epidemics are all gifts given by this means of transportation. The monks with oily hair and slippery faces, the ancient temples rebuilt by alms, the jungles with collapsed walls and excrement everywhere, may still be (quiet and secluded), hometown, I dream of traveling there.

Camping

— Yun Sun

We know that the Boy Scouts, after Mr. Baden-Powell's extreme efforts and promotion, were conceived and born with this term; in the boundless sea of people, this loyal servant was born; our Chinese Boy Scout cause is naturally undeniably immature at present, but it has been quite active in the past two years. There have been quite a few people who have written about the records of Boy Scout operations in newspapers, but the most interesting thing about its body is nothing more than camping in the spring suburbs; but a cursory inspection and a distant view of the mound-like camp from a tall building cannot understand everything it wants to let people know.

I have visited the campsite of the Girl Scouts. They use the naturally beautiful countryside, take economical, simple, and hygienic environmental things, and provide them with the temporary needs of their lives. They set up tents on the open plains, with ventilation, sunlight, rain prevention, and moisture prevention as the highest principles; as soon as they arrive at their destination, the busiest thing is the construction of the project. They hurriedly set up the tents, and the next thing is a concentrated toilet for excrement. Using four Boy Scout sticks, they successfully created a three-dimensional square on one side not far from the tents. The outside was surrounded by snow-white canvas, and there was also a short door. Outside the door was a pile of loose soil. They said: After each person defecates or urinates, covering the pit with an inch of loose soil can prevent the smell of wood chips from overflowing. Next to the toilet, two square pits two feet deep were dug. All banana peels, melon seed shells, fish bones, and meat bones were dumped in them, which was a temporary trash can, and the outside was also covered with a layer of loose soil. It was really (gold and jade on the outside, trash on the inside).

The most artistic structure is the open-air dining room. A piece of ground the same size as a square table is dug into a trench on all sides. The buttocks are on the ground, and the legs hang down. When you sit down, you can just accommodate your knees; a piece of lead painting paper is spread on the beach, and the four corners are nailed with drawing pins. From a distance, it looks like a snow-white square tablecloth; if there are many people camping, it is simply a miniature of a city restaurant; they fan the green tree branches as chopsticks, I think if they compete with foreign Boy Scouts to eat? I guarantee that the blond-haired and blue-eyed children will be helpless.

Novel

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 5: Brewing Tea to Spend the Long Night, Enjoying the End of the Year; The Title Marks the Anti-Japanese Day, the Shouts are High

Guizhi felt that her mother's words were a bit too sentimental. Old Man Zhao was an old-fashioned person, and he might not be happy, so she smiled and said, "Grandpa probably won't move out after living here for a few months. We don't have anywhere to move to. How can we not be together next year?" Old Man Zhao understood Guizhi's intention, so he picked up his wine glass and smiled, "I hope it will be as the big girl said! Big girl, don't you dislike being neighbors with old-fashioned people like us?" Guizhi smiled and said, "What are you talking about? Neighbors like you are really one in a thousand, one in ten thousand, you can't pick them out!" Old Man Zhao smiled and said, "That's good, let's live together forever." Saying that, he picked up his wine glass and raised it to Guizhi. Only then did Guizhi's heart move, and she felt that her words were a bit inappropriate, and people had caught her in the rear. But the old man had raised his glass, and she couldn't ignore him, so she had to accompany him and take a sip from the glass. Old Man Zhao was very happy tonight, talking endlessly and drinking a lot of wine. Jiang said with a smile, "Old man, you forgot what Company Commander Zhao said before he left, you can drink wine, but don't get drunk." Old Man Zhao smiled, pushed the table and stood up, nodding and said, "You are saying good neighborly words, I won't drink anymore." The Jiang mother and daughter also stood up. Old Man Zhao's face was red, and his beard was half-cocked. He crossed his hands and blocked the way, and smiled, "We agreed in advance that after eating, we will brew a pot of tea and eat New Year's snacks, you can't leave." Jiang looked at the appearance, Old Man Zhao was already a little drunk. You can't provoke a drunk person, it's better to accommodate him when something happens, so she said, "Okay, let's bother you here for a while." Old Man Zhao let the mother and daughter sit by the stove in the house, busily brewing tea and filling snack plates, and then sat down on a wicker chair a little farther away, and smiled, "Although I am an old man, I have to talk about men and women not handing things directly, otherwise, the big girl won't be willing to sit here." Eating mutton and drinking liquor makes you thirsty easily, drink. He swayed his body, opened the top cover of the iron stove, and put a large tin of hot water on it. Guizhi was afraid that he would not put it properly, so she stood up to put it for him, and he quickly stopped her with his hand and said, "Just now you said you would live with us forever, and in a moment, you will leave." (53)

Shorthand from a Car

— Huang Yingdai

Because I wanted to be early, the old man woke up early in the morning. Was he too anxious? Arriving at the station, buying a ticket and entering the train, he sat and waited for an hour. If I had known this, why did I have to get up so early!

The continuous spring rain has caused travelers to constantly curse the heavens. However, amidst the surrounding dark clouds, it was as if a ray of sunlight suddenly shot out when it was about to rain, causing all the passengers in the car to show a kind of lucky color on their faces.

In the miscellaneous luggage and travel equipment, we can make a simple analysis of the travelers! Elegant scholars going to Hangzhou to enjoy the spring; Catholics going to Sheshan to worship; Buddhist disciples going to Tianzhu to offer incense; orphans, widows, and children returning home to visit graves, each with different purposes, but I am an exception, because I am going to visit the sick!

A middle-aged woman with disheveled hair, holding a piece of paper with a few lines of words in her hand, complained to the passengers. Isn't that the mother we met in the car the last time we went to Hangzhou? Ah, this is also a skill, nothing more than begging as a business, but smart travelers saw through her tricks, and no one was willing to open their wallets, leaving her empty-handed.

Three young people suddenly dug out a deck of playing cards and played cards on top of a small suitcase. This is also a kind of pastime on the journey, which can reduce the loneliness of the journey somewhat, right?

Arriving at Xujiahui, on the platform, two teams of people walked in: one team was the "Mrs. Army," carrying yellow cloth bags and holding a lot of incense and candles; the other team was the "Black Shirt Army," wearing crosses on their chests and holding Bibles in their hands. The people were half Chinese and half Western. Burning incense and worshiping, Hangzhou and Sheshan, what's the difference!

An elderly couple, although over half a century old, the man in a brand-new gown and the woman in a cheongsam and leather shoes, whispered sweet nothings in the car, not diminishing the style of their youth in the slightest, only making the lonely travelers envious.

Songjiang has arrived, let's get off the train, shall we? Never mind! Let this idle account end halfway at the same time, shall we?

World Rare News

Can Understand a Hundred Kinds of Dialects

German linguist Dr. Rothas can understand the national languages ​​of the whole world, including ten Germanic languages, eleven Romance languages, fourteen Slavic languages, twelve East Indian Germanic languages, four West Indian Germanic languages, eleven Finno-Ugric languages, fourteen Asian languages, fifteen Indian languages, fourteen Semitic languages, eighteen African languages, six South Sea Island languages, and four American languages. Dr. Luo can speak any of the above 140 national languages ​​at will. One day, at a world conference, he changed his voice at any time and answered the representatives of more than 50 participating countries fluently, making the representatives dumbfounded. It is said that he also understands the Basque dialect, so everyone recognizes him as the leader in the field of linguistics and breaks the record of linguistics.

Italian Gas Masks

Italy has recently promoted the purchase of gas masks by its citizens. News across the nation shows cheap gas mask advertisements are commonplace everywhere. This is because when Army Chief of Staff Goshera raised the issue of national defense, there was a proposal to order citizens to prepare gas masks, which is the Fascist ideology, an idea of preparing for war, and was announced to the people in advance.

Hybrid of Cow and Pig

Frank, a merchant in New Hampshire, USA, recently gave birth to a strange beast that is neither a cow nor a pig. However, the animal that gave birth to this strange beast was a twenty-six-month-old cow, but the head and tail are still like a pig, while the body fur, toes, are completely like a cow. After the study of zoologists, it was determined that the cow was a hybrid of a cow and a pig.

Chinese Crabs to Europe

Our country's rivers and seas are full of crabs. It is said that there is a kind of hairy crab that migrates in groups across Siberia, across Russia, through Eastern Europe, and reaches German rivers. Several scholars have conducted on-the-spot investigations and personally saw crab groups migrating over mountains and ridges. The whole of Germany is now carrying out vigorous capture campaigns, and there is even a warning of "Chinese crab plainclothes troops invading Europe."

Relationship Between Sunlight and Feet

British female medical doctor Katherine Boggam recently published a novel theory. She said: The feet of people who are often fully exposed to sunlight are bound to be longer than the feet of people who wear pants and have no contact with sunlight. The reason why Scots are so long is because they wore shorts when they were young, and their legs are fully exposed to sunlight.

French King and Wine

Pope Pius XI of Rome is the person with the most wine stored in the world. His largest wine cellar is stocked with more than three thousand bottles of various wines sent from famous producing areas such as France, Italy, Spain, Germany, and Hungary, and each year they are regularly contributed by various countries.

Buffalo Drinking Dry River Water

The area around Macpherson Center in Kansas, USA, has suffered from drought for decades, and people and animals are often harmed by the scorching heat. One day, several thousand buffalo suddenly arrived in herds at the Smakshil River, and in less than four hours, they drank the river dry. This is a story from 1866. Now the old people in this place have a saying, "ox drink," which is a metaphor for people's wild drinking, which comes from this story.

Hundred Yuan Worn Shoes

Because of the lack of materials in Soviet Russia, various commodities and daily necessities are unusually expensive. Therefore, the Soviet government has a prohibited price for ordinary materials. For example, an old pair of pants is limited to 200 rubles, a pair of broken shoes is limited to 100 rubles, and a pound of white sugar and butter is limited to 15 rubles.

Zhejiang Silkworms Damaged by the Weather

(Sheng County) Farmers in various cities and villages regard sericulture as a secondary occupation, and they pay much attention to raising silkworms and planting mulberry trees. Therefore, cocoon production is still excellent. There are 70 to 80 cocoon businesses in the entire county. In recent years, due to the unfavorable weather, silkworm cocoons have had a poor harvest, and silkworm farmers have suffered losses. Last year, sericulture had already declined. This year, rural economic panic is feared, with no funds to purchase silkworm eggs and a significant reduction in the number of silkworms raised. Moreover, most are hatching local varieties retained from their own stock. In the eastern countryside, Jinxi, Pukou, Houshan, Huatang; in the southern countryside, Shangbixi, Cangyan; in the western countryside, Chongren, Ganlin; in the northern countryside, Sanjie, Macha, Shiqiao, Changle, and other areas, the number of families raising silkworms is only about 35%. After collecting the silkworm eggs, the weather was cold, causing poor development of the silkworms. Coupled with continuous rain, the early silkworms began to change after the second sleep, with symptoms of jaundice and blackening. The late silkworms also developed white muscardine, with 40% to 50% being discarded. Currently, the early silkworms in the southeast countryside are about to enter the third sleep with vigorous leaf consumption, while the late silkworms in the northwest countryside are also starting to sleep. If the weather remains sunny and warm, the spring silkworms may still have a 30% to 40% harvest. However, with the alternating sunshine and rain, silkworm farmers are generally pessimistic.

(Xin Deng) In recent years, due to the unfavorable sericulture business, although the government has been encouraging the raising of improved breeds this year, due to the scarcity of funds, they are unable to purchase the eggs. Therefore, the silkworm farmers in various villages are currently raising native breeds (i.e., the retained breeds from Yuhang, Xinchang, Zhugui, etc.) and foreign breeds (i.e., improved breeds produced for sale) separately. The number of silkworms being raised has greatly decreased. There are more people raising foreign breeds in the areas of Lutou, Pikou, and the western countryside, while the majority of people in areas like Sanxi Town and Gangkou are hatching native breeds (mostly Yuhang breeds). The weather is abnormal, with spring feeling like winter, and continuous rain for many days. The collection of silkworm eggs is uneven, and early silkworms have experienced abdominal distension and death from eating rain-soaked leaves when they were waking up from their sleep and spreading out to eat. Unhealthy silkworms differ by as much as a week in their development. The day before yesterday, the weather turned sunny and warm, and the late silkworms were about to wake up from their second sleep. However, within two days, it started raining again, and the silkworms are being greatly affected.

London Tea Market Suddenly Becomes Active

London Telegraph reports that since April, the long-depressed tea market has suddenly become active. The market prices of Indian and Javanese black tea have all risen. The Hubei and Hunan black tea that had been stockpiled for three years and had not been sold have also been completely sold out. According to general tea merchants, this change in the London tea market is quite beneficial to low-grade Chinese black tea. As for Qimen black tea, British tea merchants suffered heavy losses last year. If the mountain prices are high this year and the costs are significant, it is still difficult to be optimistic.

Free Talk

Talents of the Grand View Garden

— Gan

In earlier years, the finale act of the Grand View Garden was Granny Liu scolding the gatekeepers. That required an elderly female role to come on stage and rant (放) a torrent of abuse, only stopping after putting on her pants backward. Back then, shouting (Kill, kill, kill!) while pointing at unarmed or already disarmed people was considered a truly majestic cry. So, this male actor playing an old woman could be considered a talent.

But times have changed greatly. Now, you hold a knife in your hand, but need to shout (Freedom, freedom, freedom!) and (Openness, etc.). The finale act needs to change.

And so, talents emerge in great numbers, each with their unique skills. Coming on stage is no longer the elderly female role, but a young female role, and not just any young female role, but what the Shanghai opera advertisements call a (Jesting Female Role). This is a special kind of character. She must know how to smile charmingly and how to throw a tantrum, how to flirt and tease, and how to be glib and slick. In short, this is a young female role combined with the role of a clown. Is it the times that create heroes (or, to be proper, (beauties)), or is it the result of a beauty's years of experience?

When a beauty is said to have (many years), it naturally means a seasoned woman who has seen many men. She has already risen from a prostitute to a madam. But she still retains her charm. Although she is selling people, she also sells herself. Selling herself is easy, but selling others is more difficult. Now, there are not only unarmed people, but also… and encountering blatant rape. To cope with such an extraordinary change, one must have extraordinary talent. Think about it: the current finale act must be both war-like and peace-like, war and peace at the same time, neither surrendering nor defending, both surrendering and defending. This is a very difficult act to perform. It cannot be done without the art of half-pushing, half-yielding, and feigning shyness. Mencius said, (Giving the world to others is easy). In fact, it is not difficult to simply offer (the world) to (others) with both hands. The problem is that it cannot be done that way. So, one must cry buckets of tears, complaining in a shrill voice: If I don't jump into the fire pit, who will?

However, when a prostitute says she has fallen into a fire pit, she still wants people to rescue her. But when a madam cries about the fire pit, few people will believe her, especially since she has already declared that she is opening her arms, ready to drag everyone into the fire pit. Nevertheless, this fresh finale act is not bad at all. It's not a very special talent, that even emptying one's mind one could come up with this idea.

The elderly female role enters, the jesting female role comes out. There are indeed many talents in the Grand View Garden!

The Three Obsessions of Literary Men

— Shi Heng

Pu Songling wrote (Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio), a massive work of over five or six hundred thousand words, all about strange and bizarre stories of ghosts and foxes. The book has been circulating for over a century, and is read by women and children alike, making it one of the most popular books in Chinese literature. Since I was a child, I have often read this book, but I always felt strange: why would a literary man come up with so many strange and eccentric events? I concluded that the author was obsessed, but I could not understand exactly what kind of obsession he was under. Recently, I reread (Strange Tales) and, by chance, I finally understood. His obsession was not simple, but can be divided into three kinds: first, lust; second, greed for wealth; and third, a combined obsession with officialdom and immortality. It was because of these three obsessions that he wrote this book of five or six hundred thousand words. In his book, these spirits are expressed very clearly. And these obsessions are not only possessed by literary men like Pu Liuxian, but by most people in China, which is why this book has been popular for so long and so widely. If the psychology of the Chinese people is not completely transformed, this book will be even more popular for longer and wider. Western critics explain that the reason why people, whether male, female, old or young, like to read strange stories is because they contain (the beauty of wonder). This may not be without reason, but what seduces people in (Strange Tales) is not this beauty of wonder, but the satisfaction of these (three obsessions).

First, lust: A refined and elegant scholar, handsome and talented (this must be the author), sits alone in his study, feeling bored, extremely bored. Then he drifts into a dream. As soon as he enters the dream, a maiden comes to him, and he gazes at her (with a dignified and beautiful appearance, like a fairy), or (with the fragrance of orchids and musk, uniquely beautiful), or (her hair is low and misty, her waist is slender and surprising; jade pistils and jade flowers are not enough to describe her). Next comes (they enter the bedroom together, loving each other deeply), or (leaking wetness, staining the bed). And so, a moment of spring is never forgotten for decades, or he goes to the underworld, digs up a coffin, or waits for rebirth, reliving old love and reuniting the broken mirror, achieving his goal and then stopping. If this is not lust, what is it? I suspect that Mr. Pu must not have had a happy marriage. His own wife was like a (demon), and he could not get satisfaction in real life, so he sought heavenly fairies in his fantasies.

Second, greed for wealth. Now that he has obtained a fairy-like lover, the next obsession is to have abundant food and clothing, and to command servants. His lover is either a fox, a ghost, or a fairy, all-powerful. If they want something, they get it. So, what is so difficult about money? For example, if he marries the Dragon King's daughter, everything will not be a problem. Emerald jewels are everywhere. If his lover is a fox or a ghost, as long as (they are in harmony, then gold and silk will always fill the boxes), and the most comfortable thing is that he (does not even know where it comes from). If this is not greed for wealth, what is it? Mr. Pu was probably a poor scholar. His life was probably not very easy. Even drinking wine may have required pawning something. So, he developed a greed for wealth.

Third, obsession with officialdom and immortality. Now that he has a beautiful wife and lives without worry, the next obsession is power. In Mr. Pu's time, the most powerful thing was to be an official, which could not only let one vent one's anger, but also judge all the injustices in the world. But I suspect that Mr. Pu was a scholar who was unsuccessful in his career. He probably never even became a minor magistrate with the title of seven rank. So, he made a (Yellow Millet Dream). Overnight, he became a cabinet minister and prime minister, above all the people and below the emperor. The world says that (Yellow Millet Dream) is a satire on poor scholars, but I don't think so. It is his harsh criticism of himself. He must have really had this dream, but it was not easy to say it directly. So, he had to find a scapegoat to take the blame for him. After repeatedly reading it, one can realize that the work is not a real satire, but is entirely written out of jealousy. But the Yellow Millet Dream ultimately cannot satisfy him, but instead makes him sigh a few more times. This makes people even more upset and angry. So, he scolds the vulgar people for being blinded by greed, and comes up with an eternal method to become an immortal, looking down at all the ignorant creatures in the sky. How happy that is. And so, (he died at the age of eighty-one. When the funeral was held, people were surprised that the coffin was light. When they opened it, it was an empty coffin). Living to eighty-one years old in the human world was not enough. In the end, he still became an immortal! If this is not an obsession with officialdom and immortality, what is it? Mr. Pu's pen name is Liuxian, which probably means that.

Furthermore, from my point of view, this book of five or six hundred thousand words (Strange Tales) was written because the author suffered from these (three obsessions), and readers are probably mostly because they are suffering from these (three obsessions), which is why they like to read it so much.

Conclusion: These (three obsessions) are not only the obsessions of literary men, but the obsessions of our Chinese nation.

Random Notes from My Hometown (Continued)

— Mu Shiying

First, I went to the caretaker's house and told him to lead the way because the grave was halfway up the mountain. I wore the caretaker's large straw hat and walked in front. The road gradually sloped upwards, and towering ancient pine trees stood tall on the roadside, with branches only at the top of the trees. The tree trunks below were five arm spans thick and stood straight. A little further on, there was a row of small springs, and the large stones at the bottom of the springs were stacked together, lying there so cleverly. It was impossible to see where the water came from and where it went, only a small stone pool with water more crystal clear than water filtered by sand. The water flowed quickly, as if flowing into the stones. A little further up from the pool, there was a steep cliff, and a waterfall hung down from the cliff, like a bolt of cloth with white flowers blooming on it. Small water droplets sprayed into the air, hanging there and never falling. I was so happy that I jumped up and down, ran to the pool, lay on the ground, and stretched my mouth to the surface of the water, drinking greedily. The crystal-clear water flowed past my eyes, and looking down from the transparent surface, I could see bubbles rising one by one, hitting the stones. Such a healthy mountain spring! If there were immortal nectar and jade elixir, this would be the immortal nectar of the Queen Mother of the West in legend, right?

Running a little further up the road, there were clumps of morning glories and camellias growing under the pine tree roots. The light red little flowers stretched their heads into the sunlight, smiling slightly with their mouths open. I picked many flowers, stuck one in my hat, and stuck one on my lapel, stretching my face into the sunlight and smiling slightly with my mouth open, just like those light red little flowers.

A stone cliff blocked the way. I turned a bend, walked along the stone steps to the top of the stone wall, and my grandfather's grave was there. The caretaker had already put down the basket and set out the wine and dishes. After bowing four times in front of the grave, I went alone from the pine forest to the top of the mountain. Towering all around were such tall pine trees, and for the first time I felt my own smallness. I climbed for a long time before I climbed out of the forest. There was still a long way to go to the top of the mountain, but the sea was already close at hand. Standing there, I shouted at the top of my lungs, and all I heard was echoes from the surrounding mountains. Below my eyes was such a small piece of land, with the fields all connected together, not even half a finger's width apart. The houses all looked like ant nests. (I am the king of the world!) Thinking like that, I laughed heartily.

By the time I rolled down the mountain and got on the boat, it was already two o'clock. When I passed the Baoguo Temple, the yellow ancient temple had already hidden its face in the thin dusk. I still lay on the bow of the boat, carrying a boatload of bright moonlight, singing songs as I went back, drunk as if because the moonlight is a very intoxicating wine.

The next day, I left those people seeing me off at the bridge and returned to Shanghai. When I saw the golden dome of the Sassoon Building again, I could still hear them saying:

(When will you come back?)

Red Radish Whiskers

— Written by J.N.L.ESRENA RD, Translated by Lin Qu

Nightmares Red Radish Whiskers disliked the friends who visited his home. They disturbed him, occupied his bed, and forced him to sleep with his mother. However, besides his various faults during the day, he had a major fault at night: snoring. He snored deliberately, of that there was no doubt.

In that large house, cold even in August, stood two beds. One belonged to Gramps; Red Radish slept in the other, at the top, beside his mother.

Before falling asleep, he coughed in the blankets, clearing his throat. But perhaps it was snoring? He breathed softly, checking if his nostrils were blocked. He practiced not breathing too heavily.

But as soon as he fell asleep, he snored. It was almost a habit.

Instantly, the Gramps's wife would dig her two fingernails into the fattest part of his buttocks, drawing blood. She had carefully chosen this method.

Red Radish Whiskers' scream suddenly woke Gramps up, who asked: "What's wrong?" "He's having a nightmare," said Gramps's wife. Then, like a nanny lulling a child, she softly sang a lullaby that sounded like an Indian one. With her forehead and knees pressed against the wall, as if trying to knock it down; her hands covering her buttocks, hiding the claw marks that came with the first snore, Red Radish Whiskers fell back into a deep sleep on that large bed, at the top, beside his mother.

Is this the kind of thing we can imagine? Is this the kind of thing we can even tell people? Other children, at this age, with hearts and bodies just as pure white, are already holding communion, while Red Radish Whiskers remains a dirty child. One night, he waited too long; he didn't dare say anything. He hoped that by wriggling in bed, the discomfort would pass. How difficult! Another night, he dreamed that he was conveniently positioned next to a boundary marker, and then he naturally, soundly relieved himself in bed. He woke up. He was surprised that there was no boundary marker beside him! Gramps's wife restrained herself. She quietly, generously, like a mother, cleaned everything up. And, the next morning, Red Radish Whiskers even ate breakfast before getting out of bed, like a spoiled child. Yes, someone brought him a bowl of broth to his bed, a carefully prepared bowl of broth, and Gramps's wife secretly added a little something into the soup with a small wooden ladle. Ah! Just a little. The older brother, Felix, and the older sister, Elestine, stared at Red Radish Whiskers at the head of the bed with a sinister look, as if they were about to laugh. Gramps's wife fed her child spoonful by spoonful with a small spoon. She winked at the older brother, Felix, and the older sister, Elestine, as if saying: "Watch out! Get ready!" "Yes, Mom." (They were already anticipating his funny face when he found out. They should have invited some neighbors to join in the fun.) Finally, Gramps's wife cast a final glance at her two older children, as if asking them: "Are you ready?" Slowly, slowly, she lifted the last spoonful to Red Radish Whiskers' wide-open mouth, feeding it straight to his throat, filling him up, stuffing him, and then said to him with a mocking and disgusted look: "Ah! You dirty thing, you've eaten it, you've eaten it, you've eaten what you peed out yourself, what you peed out the night before last." "I guessed it already," Red Radish Whiskers replied indifferently, without making the funny face they had hoped to see. He was already used to it, and if we are used to something, we no longer find it strange.

Discussions

It's Your Sacrifice

— Xiao Zhi

I often hear people shouting (Self-sacrifice), and I often think that it is indeed a pleasant, beautiful, and fashionable phrase, so sometimes I half-consciously, actually unconsciously, learn to shout it too. The reason is very simple: I am a youth, I also love beauty, and I love fashion even more.

Last night, while discussing a certain issue with Gang, I again used this beautiful and pleasant term as a powerful reason, so I repeatedly shouted (I sacrifice myself) (Self-sacrifice). I even explained: (If you don’t sacrifice the small self, there will be no big self). Gang said, (It's your sacrifice) (It's your sacrifice) you are happy, you go and sacrifice yourself then. In fact, isn't it the silly children who take (you) to sacrifice that makes all of reality so lively? Naturally, the patterns would not become more novel or more fluent. ... After hearing these words, I had some understanding; I thought: Yes, (It's your sacrifice) is more reasonable and meaningful than (Self-sacrifice), and of course it is more beautiful and fashionable, and the sound of (It's your sacrifice) is also louder and more pleasant than (Self-sacrifice).

What is (It's your sacrifice)? For example, you Chinese, if you don't sacrifice a lot, how can I, Japan, occupy your Northeast? With your little people sacrificing, my young marshal will be able to afford Ford airplanes with three engines, and there will be so many gold bars for the Japanese to rob, and even if the old base is lost, there is still overseas to go; with this group after group, batch after batch of you sacrificing for me and being driven by me, then this seat should belong to me, and this power should be made by me; if you smoke opium, if you set up gambling houses, if you sell your flesh, then the virtuous and honest me can use it as a resource to make a living; other things such as, only when you die can I live, etc., are the true meaning of (It's your sacrifice), and these facts are so worthy of praise and admiration! Silly children, you may continue to insist on your (It's your) spirit and promote it, the facts will bring you more excitement and the patterns will definitely be more novel.

Literature and Art

Touring Longhua

— Gong Si

Sweetgrass competes in spring, sprouting green shoots,

Idly taking children for a stroll through Longhua.

Fragrant clothes and graceful shadows fill the Chan temple with bustle,

Watching all the offerings of Buddha flowers by the Wu people.

Students tour in spring, stepping on soft red,

Two or three crane their necks towards the east gate of the temple.

Secretly taking snapshots of people with quick cameras,

Faces can't escape the single click of the shutter.

Village girls fill the corners of the temple,

Burning incense and prostrating, aided by a pretty maid.

Bound feet love to circle the pagoda,

Only managing three stories before tiring.

Fashionable women, bare arms in a fancy car,

Short, tousled hair without needing a comb,

Also love to draw lots, joining in the merriment,

Kowtowing to the True Thusness in the Great Hero Hall.

Blue-eyed foreign consorts appreciate the spring,

Enjoying the scenery and indulging in pleasure during these fragrant days.

The east wind doesn't need mink or fox collars,

Snowy lotus roots are clearly visible.

Butterflies seek flowers, coming and going frequently,

Male and female entice each other around the brambles.

They are more aware of seeking mates,

Deliberately flying in pairs, chasing each other affectionately.

Poor Illness Diary

— Xiao Zhi

Only unity is enough for survival These past two weeks, being poor has been a real problem. But being poor is not just as simple as being hungry, because being hungry is just being hungry, and you can still move around. Sometimes, just by moving around, you might be able to temporarily fill your stomach. However, the affairs of the poor are never that simple; in reality, they play out in ways that make people scratch their heads. Isn’t the illness in these two weeks too peculiar and unpredictable? Yes, this is inevitable. From now on, I absolutely believe that (poverty) and (illness) are linked and never separate.

This afternoon, Ying came to visit me as usual. I am really grateful and happy because, as a lonely, poor, and sick traveler in a foreign land, I actually have an old friend to come and talk to. Isn’t this joyful enough? Discovered That today, my spirits are much better. She said that Tarzan the Ape Man is a beautiful film that pleases people and broadens their horizons. She suggested that I accompany her to buy two hours of happiness. I agreed to her, so we stepped onto the stairs of the Paia Theater. The plot of this film is very simple, but the picture depicts the greatness and beauty of nature, as if taking us on a two-hour tour of Africa!

At the dinner table, Ying and I talked about (Tarzan the Ape Man) again; Ying asked me, (What lessons did (Tarzan the Ape Man) give people?) I said (So many people spend all day just working on money, with their minds full of (How to get rich?) (How to get rich?) Their whole lives are buried in the eyes of copper coins! This is truly the most ridiculous and most pitiful group in the world! Look, wasn’t (Burke) full of (collecting ivory) (getting rich)? In the end, he died buried in (ivory). In fact, what could he really possess?

·········)

(Your views are really good;) she said spiritedly, (But there is one point you shouldn’t lightly overlook, which is that, in this robber world, this beastly world where there is only might and no justice, if the weak do not unite with each other, foreign insults will definitely come layer upon layer and eventually be eaten by the strong! Because of this, although (apes) and (elephants) are the weaker ones among the beasts, because they can firmly unite and work together, as a result, although the (Japanese) are fierce, they are unorganized, and eventually the (Japanese nest) is trampled flat by the elephants! In fact, our country is already extremely weak, and within the country, opinions are divided and people are killing each other, insisting on creating personal supremacy. What about the loss of the Northeast and the crisis in Pingjin? This is just a small firecracker, not enough to deafen or enlighten! Therefore, foreign insults listen to it. National demise also listens to it, fortunately, the country belongs to everyone, as long as it doesn’t hurt (my) skin. The country is like this, so there is no need to mention the premier’s words (uniting the weak nations of the world)!… But, without unity, can we survive?…

I smiled and poured her a cup of tea. I said, "Speak slowly, don't choke yourself."

The Immortality of Matter

— Yang Dehui

I don’t know who invented materialism, but our patriotic profiteers were the first to use it, no, I’m afraid it was still the non-resistance advocates who enjoyed it first. The national crisis after September 18th is becoming increasingly serious, which no one denies. However, the national crisis is still a national crisis. If the land is occupied by others, it just becomes (mine is yours, yours is mine), so what does it matter? Moreover, according to the scientific definition of matter, (matter is something that exists in space, has shape, and can be recognized and felt by people) isn’t land a thing? All things are matter, and no one will deny that the so-called (immortality of matter) is wrong. Therefore, our Young Marshal Zhang, in accordance with materialism, lost the Eastern Provinces. Although the land was occupied by others, in terms of procedure, it was just a change of management, but matter is ultimately immortal, so what’s the big deal? He held this principle, so the loss of Jinzhou, the fall of Yuguan, and the abandonment of Rehe were all predetermined ideas. I’m afraid that our common people’s scolding is due to not understanding the immortality of matter. Telegram reports how the enemy forces are and how our forces are, explaining in detail, so you can rest assured and live that cowardly life. It’s a pity that our common people still don’t understand his intentions, and they scold with righteous indignation.

It’s no wonder that our common people don’t understand the immortality of matter. Even the dignified Central Committee member Mr. Zhang Ji and the Minister of the Navy are investigating Young Marshal Zhang’s ancient paintings and the sale of the Tianjin Naval Hospital, using the government’s name to pursue the case by law. Unfortunately, they still don’t know the theorem of the immortality of matter, and Young Marshal Zhang is probably secretly laughing at them.

Although the ancient paintings of the Summer Palace were handled by Young Marshal Zhang and not handed over to the government, but taken away privately, regardless of whether they were sold to foreigners or not, ancient paintings are still ancient paintings, it’s just that they are stored abroad. So why investigate? The sale of the naval hospital is also the same principle. Young Marshal Zhang, who understands the immortality of matter, would not make any mistakes in the procedure. The government is really meddlesome.

However, the profiteers understand this principle and send large sums of money overseas. The foolish anti-treason group uses bombs and threats, but they will not make the profiteers feel alarmed, because the outflow of money does not necessarily mean that the enemies will swallow it; it is still circulating, turning into silver, gold, or copper, but the original substance is still there! (The immortality of matter,) is also the same principle, who says it isn’t! Ah, ah, foolish countrymen, smart profiteers, and Young Marshal Zhang, are all eternally famous.

Woolen Sweater

— Flood

After the graduation certificates were obtained, the faces of the students were all filled with victorious smiles.

Store Clerk Communication

Doctor's Wife

Dear Editor:

I was originally a store clerk, and I lost my job after (September 18th). Now I勉强 make do as a tutor. My wife is a woman who has never been to school, she is very loyal to me, and I love her very much. Last year, she saw that I had lost my job and my income had decreased, so to save money, she left me and returned to her hometown. She has a very close female friend who is an experienced elementary school teacher. Because her situation is very difficult, my wife used to ask me to write letters to comfort her. Therefore, the three of us became friends.

The situation of my wife's female friend is like this: She married a student from Tongji University when she had not yet graduated from normal school. The love at that time was also very good, but they separated after living together for only a month or two. After the European War, her husband went to Germany to study. At that time, because he had financial difficulties, she and her father repeatedly ran around to appeal and raise money to support him. The salary she received was even more湊入汇去. The matter is really strange, after he graduated from university, he gave her fewer and fewer letters, and the words in the letters often had a kind of disgusted expression. Writing letters to urge him to return home, he said he still needed to study. After he got his doctorate, she urged him again, but he still made excuses to postpone it. She suspected at that time that he had married a German woman abroad; her father had also written to the ambassador to Germany, asking him to urge him to return home. The reply only said that the reason he had not returned home was probably because he did not have travel expenses. Once, she wrote a letter to question him and asked to separate, but he ignored her. Since then, there has been even less correspondence. Asking people to inquire about news, but there was no result; only one or two letters were sent home a year. His mother, who is over sixty years old, is looking forward to it and has repeatedly sent letters urging him, but to no avail. This has dragged on for almost twenty years. She has neither formally divorced him, nor has she met a new lover, and her life is extremely tragic.

Last year, my wife returned to her hometown, and old friends reunited, comforting each other, and their feelings became more intense. My wife often asked her to write letters to me on her behalf. Therefore, she got to see the secrets between the two of us: she was very envious! I have repeatedly told her to officially divorce and meet a new lover. Her replies always said that divorce was not a problem at all, but the power of the old ethics was still very strong, opposing divorce and despising remarriage. Except for you, there is no one else among relatives and friends to help me. I have no hope for this life. This is so painful! I originally wanted to find her a lover among relatives and friends, but after paying attention for several years, I have not found a suitable person. In this situation, I have no choice but to write a letter to comfort her, saying: (I am willing to love you as much as I love my wife, and we can live together when we have the opportunity). Usually, we still do our own jobs as usual, our finances are independent of each other, and we help each other; we will be pioneers of a new type of male and female union to moisten her withering soul.

Dear Editor, you are a guide for people. Is it okay to do this? Please give me your honest instructions.

Wishing you good health, sincerely, Zhang Zhicheng

Editor's Note: The reason why this doctor who studied in Germany did not return home, although according to the reply from the German embassy, it was said to be because he did not have travel expenses. But from the way he treated his wife coldly, it is probably as his wife expected, nineteen times out of ten he already has a new love. Otherwise, the tuition fees in the past were still arranged by his wife and others; why is he embarrassed to ask for the last travel expenses now? Although he is said to be a dignified doctor, his personality is completely gone; we cannot help but scold him here as an (ungrateful) thing, and we advocate giving him appropriate punishment. This doctor's wife should apply to the court for a divorce and reserve the right to demand compensation for damages and alimony from him after the doctor returns home in the future. Unless he is willing to be a ghost in a foreign land, otherwise he must be held accountable.

Mr. Zhang, because he is motivated by righteous indignation, decides to moisten the doctor's wife's about-to-withered soul, which is a righteous act; however, you say that you are willing to love her as much as you love your wife, and you and you have the opportunity to live together, what do these two sentences really mean? If your union is just to help each other, then you must first discuss it with his husband's family, otherwise you may have the crime of (interfering with the family). In case your union is not only this, but also hopes to further have the name of husband and wife. Then, on his side, the divorce procedures must be completed; on your side, you must also discuss it with your wife. Otherwise, the (bigamy) crime is established.

Self-Employment Introduction

Please send submissions for this column directly to Mr. Xu Zhichao, c/o Amateur Weekly, this newspaper.

Mr. Xu Zhichao, 19 years old, from Shanghai, high school education, specializes in communication. He previously worked in a foreign company for many years. He now wants to seek a suitable position with a monthly salary of 30 to 50 yuan. Correspondence address: Zhongzheng School, No. 6 Fudeli, Wuzhen Road, Zhabei.

Mr. Chen Guyu, from Guangdong, 30 years old, graduated from an old-style middle school, knows Mandarin, and has served as an elementary school teacher and agency secretary. Novels

Fleeting Time in Dreams (Continued Thirty-Seventh)

— Qin Shouou

There was originally an organization in Nanjing calling itself the National University Professors' Association for Anti-Japanese Salvation. Wu Yi was also one of the standing committee members. However, before the Wang Guodong incident, he did not often consult on the association's affairs, at most signing his name on declarations and circulars. Therefore, he really knew nothing about the organization and achievements of this salvation association.

(It's quite a large courtyard!) Since Wu Yi was determined to do some solid salvation work, he certainly couldn't just sit at home. His first step was to visit the National University Professors' Association for National Salvation, hoping to do some practical work within the limits of an executive committee member. The association's location was No. 18 ○○ Volume. According to Wu Yi's prediction, it would be a couple of small rooms rented from someone else, just for meetings and discussions. Little did he know that when he arrived at the place, it was the complete opposite of what he expected. No. 18 turned out to be a newly built small Western-style house. A large blue banner with white characters hung prominently on the door. Besides that, there were no other signs. Undoubtedly, this was a place exclusively occupied by an organization!

Stepping inside, it was even more extraordinary. The paint was brand new, and the decoration was luxurious. If it weren't for the sign outside, Wu Yi would have almost suspected it was a golden house for important people to hide their mistresses. The house, it was said, had a reception area, a reception room, a meeting hall, staff offices, a committee member lounge, a secretary's office, a standing committee member's office, a dining hall, and so on. It had everything! Even combining the ○ big administrative office and the teaching affairs office, it still wouldn't be as complete and spacious as this place!

(You go ahead! I don't have anything to do. I'll just look around for a while and then leave!) Because Wu Yi had already registered at the reception room when he entered, the seven or eight errand runners wearing white bamboo cloth uniforms with numbered copper plates on their chests all knew that a committee member had arrived. They stood up neatly together, only stopping short of bowing and greeting him. At the same time, one errand runner with a number one copper plate led the way respectfully, leading him inside. However, Wu Yi was naturally humble and couldn't get used to such official flattery. He waved him away hastily after passing the meeting hall.

Crossing the committee member lounge, he arrived in front of the staff offices. There were two offices, one smaller one, with four exquisitely crafted desks and four large swivel chairs with backrests. The other furnishings were also more elaborate than Wu Yi's principal's office. At the moment, it was as quiet as if no one were inside. Wu Yi tiptoed over for a look and saw an old gentleman, about his own age, hunched over a desk, diligently studying Brother Xing Yuren's (Painting Bedchamber Studies). There was also an errand runner snoring like thunder in the corner accompanying him.

Seeing that both of them were sound asleep, Wu Yi didn't want to stay longer, so as not to disturb their pleasant time. He quietly retreated. (Three! Three! Three! Damn it! Another three...)

(Okay! This time it's a sure six, three, six, eighteen corners, plus four corners, together two dollars and one [Is there a foreign coin? Find it!]) He had only just reached the front of the other, larger office. A chaotic... the clinking sound of silver coins and small change crashing together pierced Wu Yi's ears, immediately arousing his curiosity. He couldn't help but take a few quick steps and step into this mysterious office.
