Film Special

The Progress of the Soviet Comedy Film Movement

— Zhu Dalin

Thirty-Two-Year-Old Young Director

Eisenstein Presides Over It

The Soviet Union is a socialist country adept at creation. Anything that benefits the people's health and spirit is vigorously promoted and encouraged. A few months ago, we heard that the country encouraged writers to engage in playwriting and turn them into motion pictures to regulate the spiritual lives of the working masses, and recently it has been steadily progressing. Isn't that admirable?

This news not only opens a new chapter in the modern film industry, but also during this time when countries around the world are declining, the sudden appearance of such a good phenomenon is really something worthy of our attention. Sergei Eisenstein, who is in charge of comedy films, is still a 32-year-old youth. He is regarded as one of the four major directors of the film movement in the Soviet Union. It is said that he does not want to hang up an empty sign, but to engage in the creation of real life. He believes that individualistic male and female actors cannot meet the requirements of the new society, so he wants to work hard for the masses. His first successful work was the play "Strike," which appeared in 1924. In this film, he used the emotions of the masses to train actors and achieve extra success. Other films he starred in include "Potemkin," "October," and "Ten Days That Shook the World."

Mary Pickford and Douglas Fairbanks visited Paris in 1927 and were deeply moved after seeing his "Potemkin." When they arrived in Moscow, they went to visit him immediately.

Eisenstein once went to Hollywood, but he returned to Moscow soon after because he was dissatisfied. At that time, he was not only the most active person in the film industry, but also had profound research on the theory and practice of film. In addition to serving as a professor at the Moscow National Film Institute, he also worked as the director of the Psychological and Health Laboratory for Studying Mass Response.

He is now making comedy films, using the most exquisite and ingenious devices to achieve satisfactory results. Harpo Marx, one of the four great comedians, recently went to Moscow to collaborate with him.

National Salvation Film Conference

— Zong

The Entire Film Industry Produces Twelve Short Films

To Fund the (Film Number) Aircraft

The Preparatory Committee for Fundraising for the (Film Number) Aircraft through Joint Film Production in the Film Industry held a script discussion meeting the day before yesterday at the Tsinghua Alumni Association on the fourth floor of the Continental Commercial Building. Attendees that day included: Municipal Government Representatives Zhu Shaoping and Shen Gao, Lianbiao Representatives Jin Yu, Bu Wancang, and Cai Chusheng, Star Representatives Zheng Zhengqiu, Hehe Representatives Wang Pengyi and Gu Wenzong, Tianyi Representatives Gao Tianqi, Hengsheng Representatives Zheng Yingshi, Jinan Representatives Yang Tianle and Xie Yuesheng, Yueming Representative Zhao Zhenbao, Dadong Representatives Gong Lusun, Xifan Representatives Ren Xifan. Around nine o'clock, they were invited to be seated for a meal by Zhu and Shen. The discussion of scripts from various companies began at ten o'clock. First, Zheng Zhengqiu spoke about the national salvation plot of students and actors. Then, Bu Wancang narrated a children's national salvation story. Next, Cai Chusheng spoke about the workers' national salvation guidelines. Then, Lusun narrated the political circles' national salvation strategies. Yang Tianle described the military personnel's national salvation preparations. Mr. Xie Yuesheng's beggars' national salvation mobilization. Zhao Zhenbao talked about the spirit that farmers should have for national salvation. Gu Wenzong narrated the final struggle of artists for national salvation. Gao Tianqi did not bring a script, but said some methods for the business community to save the country, and suggested making a story about a dancer saving the country. Ren Xifan, because he was not good at screenwriting, was willing to help with a thousand feet of newsreel of the Rehe war. Zheng Yingshi, because there were no basic actors, volunteered to shoot the opening and ending credits.

The entire project is divided into twelve plots. After the attendees modified the unreasonable parts of each plot, they discussed how to link these eleven stories together. As a result, it became more difficult, so it was finally decided to perform each story in a narrative style, with the ending summarizing the goal of this aviation national salvation campaign. At twelve o'clock, Shen Gao instructed each representative to submit their story to Mayor Wu within three days, and also asked each representative and screenwriter to think of a better way to connect the plots, and also to think of a general title for the entire film, so as to determine the overall name of the film. Mr. Shen said: (It would be best if it can be successful before the end of May.)

Finally: After all the discussions were completed, the preparatory committee was changed to the executive committee, and all company representatives automatically became executive members and started the overall work from May 1st.

Then, this national salvation film, which is made by the joint efforts of the entire film industry's directors, actors, set designers, photographers, and various personnel, will surely be able to call on the audience and have the power to influence the audience to save the country.

Audience Opinions

Criticisms from a Family of Six Regarding "The Morning of the Metropolis"

— Tang Hanguang

When "The Morning of the Metropolis" was screened at Guanghua a few days ago, our whole family (father, mother, older brother, sister-in-law, two older sisters and me, seven people in total) went to see it. Afterwards, at the dinner table, everyone expressed some comments about this film. In addition to some praise, below are some different opinions: Father, with the attitude of a family elder, expressed that it was too much for Xu Qiling not to accept the gifts and inheritance from his real father (Huang Menghua). Moreover, it is not the behavior of a good man to have this old man angered to death. Therefore, this point is quite doubtful.

Mother's opinion was that the name of Menghua's lover was not mentioned at all in the explanation, which was a loophole. The elder brother's opinion was that Qiling was innocently arrested and sent to prison, but the editor defended the court, saying that his grievances were cleared because the court conducted a thorough investigation. This clearly shows that the screenwriter is satisfied with the current court system, or he does not have the courage to attack it. In addition, Qiling told his sister in prison that (I must take revenge), but in the end, Qiling only hit Huiling a few times. This revenge is too light. The two older sisters felt that it was unreasonable for Huiling, a playboy, to wholeheartedly love the female worker Wang Renmei; it was also unreasonable for parents not to punish their son for being unruly at home; and it was also unreasonable for Menghua to find out that his son was unfilial and that Xiao Zhang was helping the abuser, so he called the servants to lock them up. It was also unreasonable that Xu Qiling came out of prison to save his sister, but his sister did not ask: (Brother, when did you get out of prison?) This is also unreasonable.

As for me and my sister-in-law, we both thought this film was very good, but it was a pity that Qiling rejected Menghua's inheritance. So I said: If I were Qiling, I would definitely accept this property. Why should I leave this money to Huiling to do evil?

"Going to Shanghai" Completely Filmed, Produced by Sanyi Company

— Zhu Yuanshi

The Rongji Sanyi Film Company, organized by Zhang Ye'er, Wang Wu Neng, and Huang Jinrong, borrowed the Lianhua studio to film "Going to Shanghai." It has been two months since then, and it was completely filmed the day before yesterday. It is also said that it will be screened at the Central Grand Theater in the near future. This film is all about persuading people to learn to read and the suffering of illiteracy, etc.

Cecil B. DeMille's Eyes Are Sharp

— Lin

Although the great director Cecil B. DeMille is old, his eyes are still sharp. None of the actors he has chosen have failed to make a name for themselves. Last year, Paramount launched a beauty pageant, and four beauties were selected as a result. Cecil B. DeMille invited these four beauties to dinner. At the dinner table, he said, (You four were selected from four thousand people. I predict that your future will be very bright. Just wait and see.)

Six months later, Cecil B. DeMille invited them to dinner again. As expected, his prediction came true, and each of them had a long-term contract and a good start. Kathleen Burke played a key role in "Island of Lost Souls" and "Murders in the Zoo". Gail Patrick also worked in the same film. Lona Andre played the leader in "The Mysterious Rider". Verna Hillie appeared in "From Hell to Heaven" and played a key female role in "Under the Tonto Rim".

Ann Harding Is Afraid of Seeing Old Men

— Hua Ming

Ann Harding of RKO, her husband Harry Bannister, is an old man of ninety. After Ann Harding married him, she was so annoyed by this old man that she was afraid of him, so except when she was filming at the company, there was no way to avoid Bannister. Everywhere else, she did not stay with him. Bannister was extremely angry and divorced her immediately. But afterwards, Bannister regretted it very much. Ann Harding was afraid that he would pester her again, so she asked RKO for leave and did not know where to hide. Later, Bannister went to look for her everywhere. He actually found her. It turned out that Ann Harding had hidden in a theater thirty miles outside of Hollywood. She used to be an actress in this theater. Now she has returned to her old place, and the theater owner is very sincere in entertaining her and inviting her to perform a play. Unexpectedly, Bannister found this theater on this day and also came in as a guest. When Ann Harding saw him in the middle of the play, she immediately ran away from the backstage.

This piece is translated from the April issue of Motion Picture magazine. Although it is not (sensual) (scented), it is also talking about men and women. I am afraid that people like Mr. Tongzhen, who are moralistic, will cite it and cost them their minds, so I will explain it at the end of the article. Anyway, everything about women is (in what era is it now?) cannot be done. In the end, I hope that all women will die, then what era (?) will not be a problem. I wonder what Tongzhen thinks? (The author is responsible for the content)

(I don’t say anything. Anyway, with the four characters "The author is responsible for the content," the editor can just publish it without even looking at the manuscript and does not need to be responsible. Not smart.)

Film Novel "Cavalcade" (8)

— Ne

Of course, the most miserable person to hear about the war was Keiin. She sighed and said, (In any case, Edward is spared this disaster. Fortunately, he died when he was happy. Otherwise, seeing the demise of this world, I don't know how much more heartbroken I would be?) When Robert heard this, he knew that she had suffered a lot and could not bear any more stimulation, so he quickly ran over to support her and said, (Why do you worry so much? We have experienced several wars before, but the world has not collapsed.) Keiin's eyes were filled with tears, and she said (The world I am talking about is my own world; my world is very small.) At this time, Keiin's attitude was different from before. She suddenly took a desperate gamble and said, (Okay! Long live England! May we always be victorious and indestructible! Joey, although you are a child, you are qualified to carry a gun and fight. Let's stake our life and death on this one throw!)

Everyone looked at her attitude and looked at each other in dismay, speechless. Keiin had made up her mind, and crazily cried and shouted, and went to another room.

In this way, their whole family joined the war. The first one was, of course, Robert, who led an army to the front line. Keiin and Margaret also joined the rear service, doing the work of rolling bandages, and they didn't know how many miles of gauze they rolled in a day. The last one was Joey, who also left Eton College and joined the army. He wore a yellow military uniform and looked like a heroic young military officer, but he also knew that danger was waiting for him in the future. So he had to seize the moment and live in the moment, so that he could put life and death out of his mind. One day, Joey and a partner went to a nightclub together. At that time, Fanni had become a red female performer, and her fame was overflowing in the mouths of Londoners. Joey didn't recognize her when he first saw her in that nightclub. He asked the people next to him who that heavenly being was, and they said that it was the extremely popular Fanni Brelgis. Joey was stunned when he heard this. He quickly looked at the playbill, and carefully recognized the face on the stage, and it was indeed Fanni Brelgis. He waited with joy until the play was over, and then ran to the backstage to see her. She didn't recognize Joey at first, and thought that this unfamiliar man had run into the actress's dressing room and wanted to drive him out. Later, after someone explained the origin, Fanni remembered her childhood friend. From then on, their love also began. Fanni gave up many princes, nobles, and wealthy merchants, and focused her love on Joey alone. Joey's good fortune is known. However, good times don't last long, and beautiful clouds are easy to dissipate. Heaven has already destined that Joey's good fortune is strong, and disaster will follow closely. (To be continued)
